[25/02/24, 4:28:52‚ÄØPM] abhay: 1) Sustainable Development Goal(water, air, soil).
2)Environmental laws & acts
[25/02/24, 4:52:33‚ÄØPM] Abhishek jha_20233504: The Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) are a set of 17 global objectives established by the United Nations in 2015 to address a wide range of social, economic, and environmental challenges. These goals are designed to promote sustainable development and improve the well-being of people worldwide by 2030. The SDGs cover a broad spectrum of issues, including poverty, hunger, health, education, gender equality, clean water, sanitation, affordable and clean energy, decent work and economic growth, industry innovation, reduced inequalities, sustainable cities, responsible consumption, climate action, life below water, life on land, peace, justice, and strong institutions.

Each goal consists of specific targets and indicators to measure progress. The SDGs recognize the interconnectedness of global challenges and emphasize the need for collaborative efforts among governments, businesses, civil society, and individuals to achieve meaningful and lasting impact. The goals also prioritize leaving no one behind, aiming to address disparities and ensure that the benefits of development reach all segments of society.

The SDGs provide a universal framework that guides countries and stakeholders in formulating policies, strategies, and actions to address pressing issues and create a more equitable, sustainable, and resilient world. As a comprehensive agenda, the SDGs inspire collective action towards a shared vision of a better future for people and the planet.

[19/01/25, 8:54:23‚ÄØAM] Abhishek jha_20233504: class Solution {
public:
    int subarraySum(vector<int>& nums) {
        int sum = 0;
        for(int i=0;i<nums.size();i++){
            int start = max(0,i-nums[i]);
            while(start!=i+1){
                sum = sum + nums[start];
                start++;
            }
        }

        return sum;
    }
};¬©Ô∏èleetcode
[19/01/25, 8:54:33‚ÄØAM] abhay: bool flag=false;
vector <int> fact(1e5+1,1);
vector <int> binfact(1e5+1);
class Solution {
int MOD=1e9+7;
inline int add(int a, int b) {
    return ((a % MOD) + (b % MOD)) % MOD;
}

inline int mul(int a,int b){
    return ((a%MOD) * 1LL * (b%MOD))%MOD;
}

int binexp(int a,int b){
    int res=1;
    while (b>0){
        if (b&1){
            res=(res*1ll*a)%MOD;
        }
        a=(a*1ll*a)%MOD;
        b>>=1;
    }
    return res;
}


void factorial(){
    for (int i=1;i<1e5+1;i++){
        fact[i]=mul(fact[i-1],i);
    }
}


void binfactorial(){
    for (int i=0;i<1e5+1;i++){
        binfact[i]=binexp(fact[i],MOD-2);
    }
}

int ncr(int n,int r){
    if (n-r<0) return 0;
    return mul(mul(fact[n],binfact[r]),binfact[n-r]);

}

public:
    int minMaxSums(vector<int>& nums, int k) {
        if (!flag){
            factorial();
            binfactorial();
            flag=true;
        }
        
        
        
        sort(nums.begin(),nums.end());
        vector<int> copy=nums;
        reverse(copy.begin(),copy.end());

        int ans=0;
        int n=nums.size();
        for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for (int j=0;j<min(k,n-i);j++){
                ans=add(ans,mul(nums[i],ncr(n-i-1,j)));
                ans=add(ans,mul(copy[i],ncr(n-i-1,j)));
            }
     }
    
        return ans;
    }
};¬©Ô∏èleetcode

[27/01/25, 1:06:03‚ÄØAM] abhay: class Solution {
    int m;
    int topology(vector<int>&visited,vector<int>&node,vector<int>&indeg,int idx){
        int count=0;
        queue<int>q;
        // for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
        //     if(indeg[i]==0) q.push(i),visited[i]=1;
        // }
       q.push(idx);
        visited[idx]=1;
        while(!q.empty()){
            auto top=q.front();
            count++;
            q.pop();
        
                indeg[node[top]]--;
                if(indeg[node[top]]==0) {
                    visited[top]=1;
                    q.push(node[top]);
                }
    


        }
        
       return m-count;

    }
public:
    int longestCycle(vector<int>& favorite) {
        m=favorite.size();
        vector<int>indeg(m,0);
        for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
            if(favorite[i]==-1) continue;
            indeg[favorite[i]]++;

        }
    
        int ans=0;
        int c=0;

        vector<int>visited(m,0);
        for(int i=0;i<m;i++){
            if(favorite[i]==-1) continue;

            if(!indeg[i]&&!visited[i]){
                c++;
                ans=max(ans,topology(visited,favorite,indeg,i));
            }
        }
        return c==0?m:ans;
    }
};

[01/02/25, 8:16:34‚ÄØPM] abhay: class Solution {
public:
    int maxFreeTime(int t, int k, vector<int>& st, vector<int>& end) {
        vector<int> ans;
        ans.push_back(st[0]);
        int n=st.size();
        for (int i=1;i<n;i++){
            ans.push_back(st[i]-end[i-1]);
        }
        ans.push_back(t-end[n-1]);
        int sum=0;
        // for (auto val:ans) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;
        for (int i=0;i<=k;i++){
            sum+=ans[i];
        }
        int curr=sum;
        for (int i=k+1;i<=n;i++){
            curr-=ans[i-k-1];
            curr+=ans[i];
            sum=max(curr,sum);
        }
        return sum;
    }
};¬©Ô∏èleetcode
[01/02/25, 8:41:38‚ÄØPM] abhay: using namespace std;

class Solution {
public:
    int maxFreeTime(int t, vector<int>& st, vector<int>& end) {
        vector<int> ans;
        multiset<int> st2;
        ans.push_back(st[0]);
        st2.insert(st[0]);

        int n = st.size();
        for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) {
            ans.push_back(st[i] - end[i - 1]);
            st2.insert(st[i] - end[i - 1]);
        }
        ans.push_back(t - end[n - 1]);
        st2.insert(t - end[n - 1]);

        vector<int> block;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            block.push_back(end[i] - st[i]);
        }

        // for (auto val:block) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;
        // for (auto val:ans) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;

        int sum = 0, k = 1; // Assuming k = 2 based on sliding window logic
        for (int i = 0; i <= k; i++) {
            sum += ans[i];
        }

        int curr = sum;
        for (int i = k + 1; i <= n; i++) {
            curr -= ans[i - k - 1];
            curr += ans[i];
            sum = max(curr, sum);
        }
        cout<<sum<<"\n";
        int res=sum;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) { // Prevents out-of-bounds for ans[i+1]
            int a = ans[i];
            int b = ans[i + 1];

            // Now ans can be a + b if we have a space of size block[i] after removing a and b
            st2.erase(st2.find(a));
            st2.erase(st2.find(b));

            if (!st2.empty() && *st2.rbegin() >= block[i]) {
                res = max(res, a + b + block[i]);
            }

            st2.insert(a);
            st2.insert(b);
        }

        return res;
    }
};

[01/02/25, 8:47:05‚ÄØPM] abhay: class Solution {
public:
    string findValidPair(const string& s) {
        vector<int> fre(10, 0);

        for (char c : s) {
            fre[c - '0']++;
        }

        for (size_t i = 0; i < s.length() - 1; i++) {
            if (s[i] != s[i + 1]) {
                int first_digit = s[i] - '0';
                int second_digit = s[i + 1] - '0';
                if (fre[first_digit] == first_digit && fre[second_digit] == second_digit) {
                    return s.substr(i, 2);
                }
            }
        }

        return "";
    }
};

public:
    bool BS1(int state,int k,long long value,vector<vector<int>>& grid){
        int n = grid.size();
        int m = grid[0].size();
        if (k >= m && state == 0) return false;
        if (k >= n && state == 1) return false;
        
        if(state==0){
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=k;j<m;j++){
                if(grid[i][j]==value){
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        }
        else{
            for(int i=k;i<n;i++){
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                if(grid[i][j]==value){
                    return true;
                }
            }
            }
        }

        return false;
    }

    bool BS3(int l,long long value,vector<long long>&search,long long sub){
        int size = search.size();
        int high = size-1;
        int low = l;

        while(high>=low){
            int mid = (high+low)/2;

            if(search[mid]-sub==value){
                return true;
            }
            else if(search[mid]-sub>value){
                high = mid-1;
            }
            else{
                low = mid+1;
            }
        }

        return false;
    }
    
         bool BS(int state,long long value,vector<long long>&search,vector<vector<int>>& grid){
        int size = search.size();
        int high = size-1;
        int low = 0;
        

        while(high>=low){
            int mid = (high+low)/2;

            if(search[mid]==value){
                return true;
            }
            else if(search[mid]>value){
                high = mid-1;
            }
            else{
                low = mid+1;
            }
        }

        cout<<low<<" ";
        cout<<high<<" ";

        if(high < 0 || high >= size) return false;

        long long x = search[high];
        cout<<x<<" ";
        long long total = value + value;
                            cout<<total<<" ";
        long long y = total - x;
                                 cout<<y<<" ";
        long long newvalue = y - x;
                                 cout<<newvalue<<" ";
        
        
        bool ans1 = BS1(state,low,newvalue,grid);
        if(!ans1){
            cout<<1<<" ";
            bool ans2 = BS1(state,high,x,grid);
            if(ans2){
                cout<<2<<" ";
                if(y%2==0){
                    cout<<y/2<<" ";

                }
                else{
                    cout<< 3;

                }
            }

                cout<< 4;
                return false;
            }
        }

        cout<<5;
        return true;

        
        
    }
    
    bool canPartitionGrid(vector<vector<int>>& grid) {
        int n = grid.size();
        int m = grid[0].size();
      
        vector<long long>searchr;
        long long totalsum = 0;
        for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
            long long sum = 0;
            for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
                sum = sum + grid[i][j];
            }
            totalsum+=sum;
            searchr.push_back(totalsum);
           
        }

        if (totalsum % 2 != 0) return false;
        
        long long value = totalsum/2;
 

        bool ans1 = BS(1,value,searchr,grid);
     

        vector<long long> searchc;
        long long totalsumc = 0;
        for(int j=0;j<m;j++){
            long long csum = 0;
            for(int i=0;i<n;i++){
                csum+=grid[i][j];
            }
            totalsumc+=csum;
            searchc.push_back(totalsumc);
        }

        bool ans2 = BS(0,value,searchc,grid);

        return ans1 || ans2;

       

        return false;

    }
};

[03/06/25, 2:42:46‚ÄØPM] abhay: class Solution {
public:
    bool canPartitionGrid(vector<vector<int>>& grid) {
        int m=grid.size();
        int n =grid[0].size();
        vector <long> rowsum(m), colsum(n);
        
        for (int i=0;i<m;i++){
            long sum=0;
            for (int j=0;j<n;j++){
                sum+=grid[i][j];
            }
            rowsum[i]=sum;
        }

        for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
            long sum=0;
            for (int j=0;j<m;j++){
                sum+=grid[j][i];
            }
            colsum[i]=sum;
        }

        
        for (int i=1;i<n;i++){
            colsum[i]+=colsum[i-1];
        }
        for (int i=1;i<m;i++){
            rowsum[i]+=rowsum[i-1];
        }

        // for (auto val:rowsum) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;
        // for (auto val:colsum) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;

        for (int i=0;i<n-1;i++){
            if (colsum[i]==(colsum[n-1]-colsum[i])) return true;
        }
        for (int i=0;i<m-1;i++){
            if (rowsum[i]==(rowsum[m-1]-rowsum[i])) return true;
        }

        if (m==1){
            for (int i=0;i<n-1;i++){
                if (colsum[i]-grid[0][0]==(colsum[n-1]-colsum[i])) return true;
                if (colsum[i]==(colsum[n-1]-colsum[i]-grid[0][n-1])) return true;
                if (colsum[i]-grid[0][i]==(colsum[n-1]-colsum[i])) return true;
                if (colsum[i]==(colsum[n-1]-colsum[i]-grid[0][i+1])) return true;

            }
        }


        if (n==1){
            for (int i=0;i<m-1;i++){
                if (rowsum[i]-grid[0][0]==(rowsum[m-1]-rowsum[i])) return true;
                if (rowsum[i]==(rowsum[m-1]-rowsum[i])-grid[m-1][0]) return true;
                if (rowsum[i]-grid[i][0]==(rowsum[m-1]-rowsum[i])) return true;
                if (rowsum[i]==(rowsum[m-1]-rowsum[i])-grid[i+1][0]) return true;

            }
        }

        if (n==1 or m==1) return false;

        unordered_map<long,long> rowmp1,colmp;
        for (int i=0;i<m;i++){
            for (int j=0;j<n;j++){
                rowmp1[grid[i][j]]++; 
                colmp[grid[i][j]]++;
            }

        }



        unordered_set<long> rowst1,colst;
        for (int i=0;i<m;i++){
            for (int j=0;j<n;j++){
                rowst1.insert(grid[i][j]);
                rowmp1[grid[i][j]]--;
                if (rowmp1[grid[i][j]==0]) rowmp1.erase(grid[i][j]);
            }
            long need1 = 2*rowsum[i]-rowsum[m-1];
            // cout<<need1<<"\n";
            // for (auto val:rowst1) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;
            // for (auto [ff,ss]:rowmp1){
            //     cout<<ff<<" "<<ss<<"\n";
            // }
            if (need1>0 and (i!=0||(grid[0][0]==need1 ||grid[0][n-1]==need1)) and rowst1.count(need1)) return true;
            if (need1<0 and (i!=m-2||(grid[i+1][0]==-need1 ||grid[i+1][n-1]==-need1)) and rowmp1.find(-need1)!=rowmp1.end()) return true;
            
        }


        for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
            for (int j=0;j<m;j++){
                colst.insert(grid[j][i]);
                colmp[grid[j][i]]--;
                if (colmp[grid[j][i]]==0) colmp.erase(grid[j][i]);
            }

            long need1= 2*colsum[i] - colsum[n-1];

            // cout<<need1<<"\n";
            // for (auto val:colst) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;
            if (need1>0 and (i!=0 || grid[0][0]==need1 or grid[m-1][0]==need1 )  and colst.count(need1)) return true;
            if (need1<0 and  (i!=n-2 || grid[0][i+1]==-need1 or grid[m-1][i+1]==-need1) and colmp.find(-need1)!=colmp.end()) return true;

        }






        return 0;
    }
};

[05/06/25, 2:17:03‚ÄØPM] abhay: template<typename T> 
class SegT{
    vector <T> maxtree;
    int n;
    public:
    SegT(int n){
        maxtree.resize(2*n);
        this->n=n;
    }
    
    void update(T val,int idx){
        int pos=n+idx;
        maxtree[pos]=val;
        pos/=2;
        while (pos>0) {
            maxtree[pos] = min(maxtree[2*pos],maxtree[2*pos+1]);
            pos/=2;
        }
    }

    
    T rangeMin(int l,int r){
        l+=n,r+=n+1;
        T res=maxtree[l];
        while (l<r){
            if (l%2) res=min(res,maxtree[l++]);
            if (r%2) res=min(res,maxtree[--r]);
            l/=2,r/=2;
        }
        return res;
    }
    
}; //zero indexed

class Solution {
 
    int cnt=0;
    unordered_map<int,vector<int>> mp;
    int n;
    void solve(int l,int r,vector<int>& nums,SegT<int> &seg){
        if (l>r) return;
        if (l==r){
            if (nums[l]!=0) cnt++;
            return;
        }

        int mini= seg.rangeMin(l,r);

        auto &idx  = mp[mini];
        // for (auto &val:idx) cout<<val<<" "; cout<<endl;

        int st= lower_bound(idx.begin(),idx.end(),l) -idx.begin();
        int end=upper_bound(idx.begin(),idx.end(),r) - idx.begin()-1;
        
        for (int i=st;i<end;i++){
            solve(idx[i]+1,idx[i+1]-1,nums,seg);
        }
        if (idx[st]!=l) solve(l,idx[st]-1,nums,seg);
        if (idx[end]!=r) solve(idx[end]+1,r,nums,seg);
        if (mini!=0) cnt++;
        

    }
public:
    int minOperations(vector<int>& nums) {
        n=nums.size();
        SegT <int> seg(n);
        for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
            mp[nums[i]].push_back(i);
            seg.update(nums[i],i);
        }
        
        
        solve(0,n-1,nums,seg);
        return cnt;

        
    }
};

[11/08/25, 6:38:29‚ÄØPM] Abhishek jha_20233504: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
const int MOD = 1e9+7;

int main() {
    ios::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(nullptr);

    int n;
    cin >> n;
    vector<long long> A(n);
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) cin >> A[i];

    unordered_map<long long, long long> freq;
    long long mask = 0;
    freq[mask] = 1; // empty prefix

    long long ans = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        for (int b = 0; b < 32; b++) {
            if (A[i] & (1LL << b))
                mask ^= (1LL << b); // flip parity
        }
        ans = (ans + freq[mask]) % MOD;
        freq[mask]++;
    }

    cout << ans % MOD << "\n";
    return 0;
}

[04/10/25, 6:46:44‚ÄØPM] abhay: #include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
#include <ext/pb_ds/assoc_container.hpp>
#include <ext/pb_ds/tree_policy.hpp>
using namespace __gnu_pbds;

template<typename T>
using pbds = tree<T, null_type, less<T>, rb_tree_tag, tree_order_statistics_node_update>;
template<typename T>
using ordered_map = tree<T, T, less<T>, rb_tree_tag, tree_order_statistics_node_update>;
#define IOS ios::sync_with_stdio(0); cin.tie(0); cout.tie(0);
#define endl "\n"

// Macros
#define int long long
#define vi vector<int>
#define vii vector<vector<int>> 
#define pb push_back
#define all(v) v.begin(), v.end()
#define sz(v) ((int)(v).size())
#define rep(i, a, b) for(int i = a; i < b; ++i)


// Constants
const int MOD = 1e9 + 7;
const int MOD2 = 998244353;
const int INF = 1e18;
const int N = 2e5 + 5;

void take(vector <int> &arr){
    int n=arr.size();
    for (int i=0;i<n;i++) cin>>arr[i];
}

bool solve2(vector<int> &arr,int n,string &ans){
    int maxi=*max_element(arr.begin(),arr.end());
    if ((n-ans.size())<(2*maxi)) return true;
    return false;
}

void solve() {
    string s; cin>>s;
    // cout<<s<<"\n";
    int n=s.size();
    vi arr(26);
    for (auto ch:s) arr[ch-'A']++;
    int maxi=*max_element(arr.begin(),arr.end());
    
    if (maxi>((n+1)/2)){
        cout<<-1<<"\n";
        return;
    }
    string ans;

    while (ans.size()!=n){
        if (solve2(arr,n,ans)) break;
        for (int i=0;i<26;i++){
            if (arr[i] and (ans.empty() or ans.back()!=i+'A')){
                ans+=i+'A';
                arr[i]--;
                break;
                
            }
        }
    }

    maxi=*max_element(arr.begin(),arr.end());
    int idx=0;
    while (arr[idx]!=maxi) idx++;
    while (ans.size()!=n){
        ans+=idx+'A';
        for (int i=0;i<26;i++){
            if (i==idx) continue;
            if (arr[i] and (ans.empty() or ans.back()!=i+'A')){
                ans+=i+'A';
                arr[i]--;
                break;
                
            }
        }
    }

    cout<<ans<<"\n";

}

int32_t main() {
    IOS;
    // #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGE
    // freopen("input.txt", "r", stdin);
    // freopen("output.txt", "w", stdout);
    // #endif
    // int t; cin>>t;
    // while (t--)
        solve();
    return 0;
}

[12/11/25, 12:13:57‚ÄØAM] abhay: ORG 0000H

MOV R7, #5          ; length of string
MOV DPTR, #STRING   ; point to string in code memory
MOV R0, #30H        ; IRAM start
MOV R2,#0H

COPY:
    MOVC A, @A+DPTR  ; read from code memory
    MOV @R0, A       ; store to internal RAM
    INC R0
    INC R2
    MOV A,R2
    DJNZ R7, COPY

;MOV SP, #60H
MOV R7, #5
DEC R7

OUTER:
    MOV R0, #30H
    MOV A, R7
    MOV R6, A

INNER:
    MOV A,@R0
    MOV R2,A
    INC R0
    MOV A,@R0
    MOV B,R2
    CJNE A,B,CHECK
    SJMP SKIP

CHECK:
    JNC SKIP
    MOV @R0,B
    DEC R0
    MOV @R0,A
    INC R0

SKIP:
    DJNZ R6,INNER
    DJNZ R7,OUTER

MOV DPTR, #8000H
MOV R0, #30H
MOV R7, #5

COPY_TO_XRAM:
    MOV A,@R0
    MOVX @DPTR,A
    INC R0
    INC DPTR
    DJNZ R7,COPY_TO_XRAM

HERE:
    SJMP HERE

ORG 4000H
STRING: DB 'ZYTIM',00

END
